# REST API JSON Payload Documentation

## GET /api/contracts - Retrieve Contract List

### Request Payload (Query Parameters)
```json
{
  "pageNumber": 1,
  "pageSize": 10,
  "sortBy": "dateAdded",
  "sortDirection": "desc",
  "filters": {
    "companyIds": ["10635467", "10558784"],
    "contractTypes": ["Signed Contract", "Amendment to contract", "Draft Contract"],
    "serviceIds": [1184, 1616, 2055],
    "siteIds": [172208, 172212],
    "dateRange": {
      "startDate": "2025-01-01",
      "endDate": "2025-12-31"
    },
    "contractStatuses": ["Active", "Expired", "Pending", "Terminated"],
    "securityLevels": [10, 20, 30],
    "searchTerm": "test"
  }
}
```

### Success Response Payload
```json
{
  "data": {
    "contracts": [
      {
        "contractId": 139996729,
        "contractNumber": "CON-2025-001",

        "company": {
          "companyId": "10635467",

        "currentSecurity": "10",
        "securityLevel": "Standard"
      }
    ],
    "summary": {
      "totalContracts": 2,
      "byStatus": {
        "active": 2,

        "terminated": 0

  "errorCode": null
}
```

### Error Response Payload
```json
{
  "data": null,
  "isSuccess": false,
  "message": "Invalid company ID provided",
  "errorCode": "INVALID_COMPANY_ID"
}
```

## POST /api/contracts - Create New Contract

### Request Payload
```json
{
  "contractName": "Annual Service Agreement 2025",
  "contractType": "Signed Contract",
  "companyId": "10635467",
  "serviceIds": [1184, 1616],
  "siteIds": [172208, 172212],
  "startDate": "2025-09-01",
  "endDate": "2026-08-31",
  "totalValue": 35000.00,
  "currency": "USD",
  "paymentTerms": "Net 30",
  "securityLevel": 10,
  "contractDocument": {
    "fileName": "annual_service_agreement_2025.pdf",
    "fileData": "base64EncodedFileData",
    "documentType": "Main Contract"
  },
  "terms": {
    "autoRenewal": true,
    "renewalPeriod": 12,
    "cancellationNotice": 60
  },
  "createdBy": 15
}
```
